-=[ Mother's Day poem ]=-  5/99


   H A P P Y    M O T H E R' S    D A Y    1 9 9 9

             ____          |\ /|
           .'    `".       | Y | is for the million things she gave me,
          / |       \       ___
         |   \__.-, (_,    /   \
          \ /`   9 `\ /    \___/ means only that she is growing old,
    ,_     )| 9 .   |`     _____
     \'.  '.\  ,_/  /        |
     _\ \.--.'.___.' `'.     |   is for the tears she shed to save me,
  .-' _`  a  \.--, .'   |
  `""` \ a K  ; ,-'\ _.;_  |___|
        '.__,. (__.'`-._ ) |   | is for her heart of purest gold;
         (_/\ '-.     /_    ___
             ;-._)-._/ _)  |__  
            /        `` \  |___  is for her eyes, with love-light shining,
            '-._______.-'   ___
               |_ |_ |     |___)
               |  |  |     |   \ means right, and right she'll always be,
               |__;__/
            .-"'-'|--\     Put them all together, they spell "MOTHER",
           '.___,_|""|     A word that means the world to me.
         jgs      \__/                                 -Howard Johnson

-=[ akeru ]=-  5/98
-supernatural lions who guarded the gattes of sunset and sunrise,
according to Egyptian mythology.  Between them ran the dark passage
of the underworld, through which the sun must pass each night.
Also known as Xerefu and Akeru; or Sef and Tuau, the Lions of
Yesterday and Today.  This two headed form was regarded as a
symbol of Time (like the Janus/Jana in Rome)

-=[ Pirate flag of Henry Avery ]=-  10/97

   In the 1600s, the skull and crossbones were
 commonly used to represent death, and it was
 adopted by pirates toward the end of the

 century.  However, the skull and crossbones
 was not a standard pirate emblem; every
 pirate had his own particular Jolly Roger
 design.
